[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1468[0m[39m:    cmsBool  First = TRUE;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1469[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1470[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlut == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return NULL;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Analysis  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash originates from dereferencing a NULL `cmsStage* mpe` in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmslut.[0m[1;92mc:1230[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `EmitCIEBasedDEF` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsps2.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `mpe = Pipeline->Elements` can be NULL when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe pipeline has no stages [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., empty or null‐duplicated pipeline[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no guard before calls to `[0m[1;35mcmsStageInputChannels[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, leading to the null-pointer deref.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The proper fix is to bail out of `EmitCIEBasedDEF` early when the pipeline or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits first stage is NULL, avoiding any dereference of `mpe`.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location and Scope  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `src/cmsps2.c`  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Function: `EmitCIEBasedDEF` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m760[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. At the very beginning of `EmitCIEBasedDEF`, insert a NULL‐check for the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Pipeline` pointer and its `Elements` member. If either is NULL, return failure [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`FALSE`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m immediately.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. No other callers, harness code, or external libraries are modified. This [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserves existing logic and simply avoids crashes on malformed or empty pipelines.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Example Patch  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```diff[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   --- a/src/cmsps2.c[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   +++ b/src/cmsps2.c[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   @@ [0m[1;36m-740[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m +[0m[1;36m740[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m11[0m[39m @@ static[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   cmsBool [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsIOHANDLER* m, cmsPipeline* Pipeline[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       cmsStage* mpe;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   +   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Guard against empty or uninitialized pipeline to avoid null-deref in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcmsStageType[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   +   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline == NULL || Pipeline->Elements == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   +       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m No stages to emit, fail gracefully.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   +       return FALSE;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   +   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       mpe = Pipeline->Elements;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing logic follows[0m[33m...[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By returning `FALSE`, `EmitCIEBasedDEF` signals failure to its caller [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`WriteInputLUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which then frees resources and aborts CSA generation without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashing.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimal change directly addresses the null-pointer dereference without [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering higher-level logic or expected output for valid pipelines.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It avoids modifying low-level accessors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`cmsStageType`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or the fuzzer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Under normal operation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon-empty pipelines[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the new check is bypassed and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting behavior is unaffected.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In fuzzed or malformed cases [0m[1;39m([0m[39mempty/NULL pipelines[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it gracefully fails [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of crashing.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side Effect: For an empty pipeline, CSA generation is aborted, resulting in no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPostScript CSA output [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturning zero bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: This behavior is acceptable for malformed input; downstream code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready handles errors after a FALSE return from `EmitCIEBasedDEF`.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid pipelines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith at least one stage[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are processed exactly as before.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invalid or empty pipelines no longer crash, improving robustness under [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No tests or harness modifications are required; existing test suite and fuzz [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrunner continue to operate as before.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. References  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar null guards exist in other parts of the code [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`cmsStageSampleCLut16bit` checks for `mpe == NULL`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns with the codebase style of defensive checks in public API layers.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo external dependencies or harness changes are introduced. This patch fully [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremedies the AddressSanitizer-detected null-deref while preserving all intended [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&InputFormat, &OutFrm, &dwFlags[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m905[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m906[0m[39m:            rc = [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, DeviceLink, Intent, [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&BlackPointAdaptedToD50[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m907[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDeviceLink[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;            [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/cmsps2.[0m[1;92mc:1065[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1070[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1065[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Read the lut with all necessary conversion stages[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1066[0m[39m:        lut = [0m[1;35m_cmsReadInputLUT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhProfile, Intent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1067[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlut == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m goto Error;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1068[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1069[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1070[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Tone curves + matrix can be implemented without any LUT[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Strengthen EmitCIEBasedDEF in src/cmsps2.c:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Currently, we only guard against a completely empty pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[33mPipeline[0m[39m==NULL [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor Pipeline->[0m[33mElements[0m[39m==NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at the top. However, EmitCIEBasedDEF walks the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpipeline twice:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m First, it tests the initial stage’s type: if it is a curve‐set, it emits [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDecodeDEF and advances mpe = mpe->Next.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Second, it immediately calls [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m again to detect a CLUT [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstage—even if mpe is now NULL. This second unguarded call triggers the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull‐dereference when the pipeline had exactly one stage.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify both cmsStageType checks so they only execute when mpe is non‐NULL:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     * Change:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCurveSetElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       to:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCurveSetElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     * And change:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       to:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This prevents any [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m call, skipping the CLUT emission path if [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno stage remains.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add an early‐reject in WriteInputLUT in src/cmsps2.c:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After duplicating and optimizing the pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`DeviceLink = [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcmsPipelineDup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mv->Lut[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; … [0m[1;35m_cmsOptimizePipeline[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensure the resulting [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDeviceLink actually contains at least one stage before calling EmitCIEBasedDEF:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         DeviceLink = [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineDup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mv->Lut[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDeviceLink == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m New guard:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDeviceLink->Elements == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDeviceLink[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mcmsDeleteTransform[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return FALSE;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35m_cmsOptimizePipeline[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         rc = [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This stops an empty‐stage pipeline from ever reaching EmitCIEBasedDEF.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional but recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Guard GenerateCSA in src/cmsps2.c:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Right after reading the input LUT [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`lut = [0m[1;35m_cmsReadInputLUT[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, validate [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat the pipeline has stages. If it doesn’t, bail out:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         lut = [0m[1;35m_cmsReadInputLUT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhProfile, Intent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlut == NULL || lut->Elements == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m goto Error;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures all downstream paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding the matrix‐shaper vs. CLUT [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranches[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m start from a valid pipeline.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExplanation:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By guarding every cmsStageType invocation against a NULL pointer, we directly [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminate the AddressSanitizer null‐dereference in cmsStageType [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmslut.[0m[1;92mc:1230[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Early‐rejecting empty pipelines in WriteInputLUT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand optionally in GenerateCSA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoids invoking EmitCIEBasedDEF on invalid data, preserving the intent of refusing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed or degenerate pipelines.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These checks do not alter the logic for normal, well‐formed pipelines: valid [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpipelines still produce the same PostScript output. In error scenarios [0m[1;39m([0m[39mempty or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle‐stage pipelines not suited for CSA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the functions now return FALSE, leading[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGenerateCSA to clean up and report failure rather than crash.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach localizes the fix to our code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsps2.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without touching external [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries, harness code, or tests. It keeps existing functionality intact while [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfully eliminating the segfault.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
